make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:3:# 1. Filter for words that:
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:4:#    - Start with a letter: ^[A-Za-z]
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:5:#    - Are only alphanumeric: [A-Za-z0-9]*$

make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:7:grep -E '^[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9]{2,}$' words_filtered.txt | shuf -n 50 > usernames.txt
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:9:# 2. Generate 50 passwords (12 chars, alphanumeric, no spaces)
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:10:> passwords.txt
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:11:for i in {1..50}; do
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:12:    pass=$(head /dev/urandom | tr -dc A-Za-z0-9 | head -c 12)
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:13:    echo "$pass" >> passwords.txt
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:14:done
make-credentials-seed-sql.sh:16:echo "Generated valid usernames (starts with letter, alphanumeric) and passwords."

GameCombat.java:216:	public static void updateWave() {
GameCombat.java:217:		if (remainingInWave <= 0 && swimmingFishes.isEmpty()) {
GameCombat.java:218:			// if the wave is done, move to next wave
GameCombat.java:219:			wave++;
GameCombat.java:220:			remainingInWave = wave * 25;
GameCombat.java:221:			secPerChar = Math.max(0.1, STARTING_FISH_SPEED - ((wave - 1) * 0.25));
GameCombat.java:222:		}
GameCombat.java:223:	}
GameCombat.java:225:	public void handleCharacterInput(int userID, char typed) {
GameCombat.java:226:		Iterator<ActiveFish> it = swimmingFishes.iterator();
GameCombat.java:227:		while (it.hasNext()) {
GameCombat.java:228:			ActiveFish f = it.next();
GameCombat.java:229:			if (f.word.charAt(f.lettersTyped) == typed) {
GameCombat.java:230:				// if you typed the next letter
GameCombat.java:231:				if (f.lettersTyped + 1 == f.word.length()) {
GameCombat.java:232:					// if you typed the last letter of the word
GameCombat.java:233:					f.lettersTyped += 1;
GameCombat.java:234:					// Update Stats
GameCombat.java:235:					lastFish = new ActiveFish(f.type, f.word, f.lane, f.x);
GameCombat.java:236:					
GameCombat.java:237:					gold += f.type.coins; 
GameCombat.java:238:					kills += 1;
GameCombat.java:239:					totalChars += f.word.length();
GameCombat.java:241:					// Record specific fish kill in DiscoveredFishes
GameCombat.java:242:					updateDiscoveredFishes(userID, f.type.id);
GameCombat.java:244:					remainingInWave -= 1;
GameCombat.java:245:					
GameCombat.java:246:					// remove completed fish from list
GameCombat.java:247:					it.remove();
GameCombat.java:248:				}
GameCombat.java:249:			} else {
GameCombat.java:250:				// if you did not type the next letter
GameCombat.java:251:				f.lettersTyped = 0;
GameCombat.java:252:			}
GameCombat.java:253:		}
GameCombat.java:254:	}
GameCombat.java:256:	public static boolean moveFishesAndCheckStickmanCollision(int userID, int pondID) {

GameCombat.java:258:			// check stickman collision
GameCombat.java:259:			if (f.x < STICKMAN_COL + STICKMAN_WIDTH) {

GameCombat.java:261:				saveResults(userID, pondID, gold, kills, totalChars, startTime, wave);
GameCombat.java:262:				return true; 
GameCombat.java:263:			}
GameCombat.java:264:			
GameCombat.java:265:			// move this fish
GameCombat.java:266:			f.x -= 1;	
GameCombat.java:267:		}
GameCombat.java:268:		
GameCombat.java:269:		// stickman was not touched
GameCombat.java:270:		return false;
GameCombat.java:271:	}
GameCombat.java:273:	public static FishType getRandomFishType() {
GameCombat.java:274:		FishType selected = null;
GameCombat.java:276:		float dice = new Random().nextFloat() * totalSpawnRateWeight;
GameCombat.java:278:		float cumulative = 0;
GameCombat.java:279:		for (FishType ft : fishSpecies) {
GameCombat.java:280:			cumulative += ft.spawnRate;
GameCombat.java:281:			if (dice <= cumulative) {
GameCombat.java:282:				selected = ft;
GameCombat.java:283:				break; 
GameCombat.java:284:			}
GameCombat.java:285:		}
GameCombat.java:287:		return selected;
GameCombat.java:288:	}
GameCombat.java:290:	public static void spawnFishIfPossible() {
GameCombat.java:291:		if (numFishMovesBeforeNextSpawn > 0) {
GameCombat.java:292:			// if must wait a number of moves before spaqn
GameCombat.java:293:			numFishMovesBeforeNextSpawn -= 1;
GameCombat.java:294:			return;
GameCombat.java:295:		}
GameCombat.java:298:		// if you have waited a number of moves, you can now spawn a fish
GameCombat.java:299:		if (remainingInWave > swimmingFishes.size() && !fishSpecies.isEmpty()) {
GameCombat.java:300:			// if the wave still has a fish to spawn
GameCombat.java:301:			FishType selected = getRandomFishType();
GameCombat.java:303:			String word = dictionary.get(new Random().nextInt(dictionary.size()));
GameCombat.java:304:			int spawnX = screenWidth - RIGHT_MARGIN - (selected.head.length() + word.length() + selected.tail.length());
GameCombat.java:306:			// check if a fish can spawn on this lane
GameCombat.java:307:			boolean clear = true;
GameCombat.java:308:			for (ActiveFish f : swimmingFishes) {
GameCombat.java:309:				int spawnFishLeftX = spawnX;
GameCombat.java:310:				int thisFishRightX = f.x + f.getFullWidth();
GameCombat.java:311:				if (f.lane == currentSpawnLane && spawnFishLeftX - thisFishRightX < MIN_FISH_GAP) {
GameCombat.java:312:					// if a fish is blocking this lane
GameCombat.java:313:					clear = false;
GameCombat.java:314:				}
GameCombat.java:315:			}
GameCombat.java:316:			if (clear) {
GameCombat.java:317:				// if a fish can spawn
GameCombat.java:318:				swimmingFishes.add(new ActiveFish(selected, word, currentSpawnLane, spawnX));
GameCombat.java:319:				
GameCombat.java:320:				// wait again a number of moves, after spawning a fish
GameCombat.java:321:				numFishMovesBeforeNextSpawn = new Random().nextInt(Math.max(4, 10 - wave) + 1);
GameCombat.java:322:				currentSpawnLane = new Random().nextInt(LANE_COUNT);
GameCombat.java:323:			} 
GameCombat.java:324:		}
GameCombat.java:325:	}
GameCombat.java:327:	public static boolean updateCombat(int userID, int pondID) {
GameCombat.java:328:		boolean isDead = false;
GameCombat.java:330:		updateWave();
GameCombat.java:331:		now = System.currentTimeMillis();
GameCombat.java:332:		if (now - lastTick > (secPerChar * 1000)) { 
GameCombat.java:333:			// if the fishes must now move based on speed
GameCombat.java:334:			isDead = moveFishesAndCheckStickmanCollision(userID, pondID);
GameCombat.java:335:			spawnFishIfPossible();
GameCombat.java:337:			lastTick = now;
GameCombat.java:339:		}
GameCombat.java:340:		sec = Math.max(1, (now - startTime - pausedTime) / 1000);
GameCombat.java:341:		wpm = (totalChars / 5.0) / (sec / 60.0);
GameCombat.java:343:		return isDead;
GameCombat.java:344:	} 
GameCombat.java:346:	public static void start(Screen screen, int userID, int pondID) {
GameCombat.java:347:		setFullscreenWidth(screen);
GameCombat.java:348:		syncFromDatabase(pondID);
GameCombat.java:349:		resetCombat();
GameCombat.java:351:		boolean isDead = false;
GameCombat.java:352:		try {
GameCombat.java:353:			while (!isDead) {
GameCombat.java:354:				isDead = updateCombat(userID, pondID);
GameCombat.java:355:			}
GameCombat.java:356:		} catch (Exception error) {
GameCombat.java:357:			error.printStackTrace();
